 					var translationObjArr = translationObjPath.split('.');
 					if(translationObjArr.length > 1){
 					    var localizedText = window.pl_js_l10n_obj[translationObjArr[0]] === undefined ? defaultText :window.pl_js_l10n_obj[translationObjArr[0]][translationObjArr[1]];
 						return localizedText === undefined ? defaultText : localizedText;
 					}else{
 						return defaultText;
 					}
 				}

    <script type="text/javascript">
     jQuery( document ).ready( function($) {
 			
 				$("#pl_widget-mortgageCalc--submit").live("click", function(e){
 					var data = {};
 					var M,P,n,r,dp;
 					var $form = $(this).closest('form');
 
 					e.preventDefault();
 					$.each($(this).closest('form').serializeArray(), function(i, field) {
 						// strip non-numbers from entered values
 						data[field.name] = field.value.replace(/[^0-9\.]+/g, "");
 					});
 
 					M = parseFloat(data.price) ? parseFloat(data.price) : function () { alert('You must enter a number for the price (rather then a word)'); return false; }()
 					n = parseInt( data.term ) * 12;
 					r = parseFloat( data.rate ) / 1200;
 					dp = 1 - parseFloat( data.down ) / 100;
 					M = M * dp;
 					
 					P = ( M*( r*Math.pow(1+r,n) ) ) / ( Math.pow( 1+r,n )-1 ); 
 					
 					if(!isNaN(P)) {
 
 
 
 						if (typeof window.PL_UTIL !== 'undefined' && PL_UTIL.formatCurrency) {
 							data.payment = PL_UTIL.formatCurrency(P.toFixed(2))
 						} else {
 							data.payment = P.toFixed(2);
 						}
 						var $inputField = $("#pls_Payment input");
 						if ($inputField.length) {
 							$inputField.val(data.payment);
 						} else {
 							$("#totalPayment").html(data.payment);
 						}
 					} else {
 						alert('There was an error, please check your values.');
 					}
 					if (typeof _placester.uii === 'object') {
 						var form_uii = $form.data('uii');
 						_placester.uii.send({
 							event: form_uii,
 							interaction_data: {
 								action: "submit",
 								element_data_type: "target",
 								element_data: _placester.uii.getElementData($form.get(0))
 							},
 							form_data: data
 						});
 					}
 				});
 				
 			});
    </script>
   </div>
